## PivotItem.Value property

Gets the value of the pivot item

```csharp
public object Value { get; }
```

            workbook.CalculateFormula();
            var worksheet2 = workbook.Worksheets[0];
            var pivottable0 = worksheet2.PivotTables[0];
            pivottable0.RefreshData();

            int pageCount = pivottable0.PageFields.Count;
            PivotField tempField = null;
            for (int i = 0; i &lt; pageCount; i++)
            {
                tempField = pivottable0.PageFields[i];
                Console.WriteLine(tempField.Name + &quot;  &quot; + tempField.ItemCount);
                for (int j = 0; j &lt; tempField.ItemCount; j++)
                {
                    if (tempField.Name.Equals(&quot;Execution Type&quot;) &amp;&amp; (string)tempField.PivotItems[j].Value == &quot;Electronic&quot;)
                    {
                        tempField.CurrentPageItem = (short)j;
                        break;
                    }
                    if (tempField.Name.Equals(&quot;Is UST&quot;) &amp;&amp; (bool)tempField.PivotItems[j].Value == true)
                    {
                        tempField.CurrentPageItem = (short)j;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            pivottable0.CalculateData();
            workbook.Save(Constants.PivotTableDestPath + &quot;net43473.xlsx&quot;);

            Assert.AreEqual(&quot;D: 30y&quot;,worksheet2.Cells[&quot;A8&quot;].StringValue);
            Assert.AreEqual(&quot;C: 7-10y&quot;,worksheet2.Cells[&quot;A10&quot;].StringValue);
            Assert.AreEqual(&quot;TRUE&quot;,worksheet2.Cells[&quot;B2&quot;].StringValue);
            Assert.AreEqual(&quot;Electronic&quot;,worksheet2.Cells[&quot;B3&quot;].StringValue );
            pivottable0.RefreshDataOnOpeningFile = false;

            var worksheet3 = workbook.Worksheets[1];
            var pivottable1 = worksheet3.PivotTables[0];
            pivottable1.RefreshData();

            pageCount = pivottable1.PageFields.Count;
            for (int i = 0; i &lt; pageCount; i++)
            {
                tempField = pivottable1.PageFields[i];
                Console.WriteLine(tempField.Name + &quot;  &quot; + tempField.ItemCount);
                for (int j = 0; j &lt; tempField.ItemCount; j++)
                {
                    if (tempField.Name.Equals(&quot;Execution Type&quot;) &amp;&amp; (string)tempField.PivotItems[j].Value == &quot;Voice&quot;)
                    {
                        tempField.CurrentPageItem = (short)j;
                        break;
                    }
                    if (tempField.Name.Equals(&quot;Is UST&quot;) &amp;&amp; (bool)tempField.PivotItems[j].Value == true)
                    {
                        tempField.CurrentPageItem = (short)j;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            workbook.Save(Constants.PivotTableDestPath + &quot;net43475.xlsx&quot;);
            pivottable1.CalculateData();
           
            Assert.AreEqual(worksheet3.Cells[&quot;B1&quot;].StringValue, &quot;Voice&quot;);
            Assert.AreEqual(worksheet3.Cells[&quot;B2&quot;].StringValue, &quot;TRUE&quot;);
            pivottable1.RefreshDataOnOpeningFile = false;
            var listobject0 = worksheet1.ListObjects[0];
            //listobject0.AutoFilter.Sorter.Sort();
            var listobject1 = worksheet0.ListObjects[0];
            //listobject1.AutoFilter.Sorter.Sort();
            workbook.CalculateFormula();
        }
